59:["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7","children":["LLM (Large Language Model) service vendor like OpenAI takes a lot of type level mistakes when composing the arguments of function calling or structured output. Even though target schema is super simple like ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"Array<string>"}]," type, LLM often fills it just by a ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"string"}]," typed value."]}]
5a:["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7","children":["In my experience, OpenAI ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"gpt-4o-mini"}]," (",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"8b"}]," parameters) is taking about 70% of type level mistakes when filling the arguments of function calling to Shopping Mall service. To overcome the imperfection of such LLM function calling, ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"typia.llm.application<App, Model>()"}]," function embeds ",["$","$L1b",null,{"href":"/docs/validators/validate","prefetch":"$undefined","className":"x:focus-visible:nextra-focus x:text-primary-600 x:underline x:hover:no-underline x:decoration-from-font x:[text-underline-position:from-font]","children":["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"typia.validate<T>()"}]}]," function for the validation feedback strategy."]}]
5b:["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7","children":"The key concept of validation feedback strategy is, let LLM function calling to construct invalid typed arguments first, and informing detailed type errors to the LLM, so that induce LLM to emend the wrong typed arguments at the next turn. In this way, I could uprise the success rate of function calling from 30% to 99% just by one step validation feedback. Even though the LLM is still occurs type error, it always has been caught at the next turn."}]
5c:["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7","children":["For reference, the embedded ",["$","$L1b",null,{"href":"/docs/validators/validate","prefetch":"$undefined","className":"x:focus-visible:nextra-focus x:text-primary-600 x:underline x:hover:no-underline x:decoration-from-font x:[text-underline-position:from-font]","children":["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"typia.validate<T>()"}]}]," function creates validation logic by analyzing TypeScript source codes and types in the compilation level.
